			}
			add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score

	}

@correct_culture_primary_score = 100
@better_than_the_alternatives_score = 50
@always_primary_score = 1000

			add = @correct_culture_primary_score

			limit = {
				culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_aegean }
			}
			add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
		}
	}

@always_primary_score = 1000

@correct_culture_primary_score = 100
@better_than_the_alternatives_score = 50
@always_primary_score = 1000

e_doria = {
	color = { 255 23 12 }
	
	capital = c_khanoia
	
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = culture:proto_greek
					culture = culture:dorian
				}
			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_hellenic }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_thracian }
				}
			}
			add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
		}
	}

@always_primary_score = 1000

@correct_culture_primary_score = 100
@better_than_the_alternatives_score = 50
@always_primary_score = 1000

e_hattusa = {
	color = { 31 15 41 }
	
	capital = c_hattusha
	
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = culture:tarhuntassan
					culture = culture:kizzuni
					culture = culture:nesili
					culture = culture:neohittite
					culture = culture:ishuwan
					culture = culture:hattian
					culture = culture:hapallan
					culture = culture:palaic
				}
			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_luwian }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_hattian }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_hurrian }
				}
			}
			add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
		}
	}

@correct_culture_primary_score = 100
@better_than_the_alternatives_score = 50
@always_primary_score = 1000

e_kemet = {
	color = { 224 165 12 }
	
	capital = c_waset #Perhaps relocate dynamically?
	
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = culture:lower_egyptian
					culture = culture:middle_egyptian
					culture = culture:upper_egyptian
					culture = culture:hyksos
					culture = culture:temehu
					culture = culture:iunetic
					culture = culture:medjay
				}
			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_kemetic }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_libyan }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_nubian }
				}
			}
			add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
		}
	}

@always_primary_score = 1000

			}
			add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score

@always_primary_score = 1000

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = culture:proto_thracian
					culture = culture:bryges
					culture = culture:tyrsenian
				}
			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_thracian }
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_aegean }
				}
			}
			add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
		}
	}
